if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'a7a54c2ee8e340cf371c2f3a0913ce73dbcfeca7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'a7a54c2ee8e340cf371c2f3a0913ce73dbcfeca7') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '87abccb6403596aa058738230f43a961d23b4930') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'a7a54c2ee8e340cf371c2f3a0913ce73dbcfeca7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt') != '9bcdc18143373e8d8ccd924223850ec6aa99efe7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt') !== '9bcdc18143373e8d8ccd924223850ec6aa99efe7') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt') !== 'ff463196e5ccf18c25bcc07254739c86ee3adf1a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt') !== '9bcdc18143373e8d8ccd924223850ec6aa99efe7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/path_functions.txt');
		}
	}
}
